                                    1005              *    8-MAR-1995  M. Durket
                                    1006              *      Changed test in ZAPNET to make sure that the file name
                                    1007              *      doesn't just consist of only a '%' sign (because that
                                    1008              *      caused WYLBUR to failsoft later in the NET module). If
                                    1009              *      the filename is just '%' and nothing more, treat it as if
                                    1010              *      it were not a network filename.
                                    1011              *
                                    1012              *    1-JUL-1997 M. Durket
                                    1013              *      Added support for using WINGS to do ACTIVE file recovery.
                                    1014              *      To activate this, we'll need to turn it on in the SIGN
                                    1015              *      module. For now, ACTIVE file SAVEs via WINGS are turned off,
                                    1016              *      but USEs (for AUTO USE at logon time) are turned on since
                                    1017              *      it's no big deal if they don't work.

0                                  10767              *
                                   10768              *
                                   10769              *  PASSOPEN - WE NEED PASSWORD TO OPEN THIS FILE
                                   10770              *
                                   10771              *  THIS ROUTINE ASKS USER FOR (MAINFRAME) PASSWORD.  IF USER
                                   10772              *  KNOWS PASSWORD, WE WILL TRY AGAIN TO OPEN FILE WITH
                                   10773              *  PASSWORD=OK OPTION.  THIS ROUTINE APPLIES ONLY TO WINGS
                                   10774              *  FILE SYSTEM.
                                   10775              *
                                   10776              *  ON ENTRY:
                                   10777              *  'NOT YOURS' MSG IS TSEG'D.  WE DECIDE WHETHER TO PURGE
                                   10778              *  OR PRINT TSEG'D MSG BELOW.
                                   10779              *
                                   10780              *  NOTE:
                                   10781              *  IF 'SET ACCOUNT ... PASS ...' OWNS DATA SET WE DO NOT
                                   10782              *  ISSUE ERROR MSG, AND DO *NOT* PROMPT FOR PASSWORD.
                                   10783              *
                                   10784              *  NOTE:
                                   10785              *  IF NO ACCOUNT ASSOCIATED WITH THE DATA SET, THEN
                                   10786              *  WE PROMPT FOR THE ACCOUNT GS.WYL.  WHICH ONLY SYSTEMS
                                   10787              *  TYPES CAN GUESS.  YES!
                                   10788              *

0                                  14466              *
                                   14467              *
                                   14468              *  OSRENAME
                                   14469              *
                                   14470              *
                                   14471              *  MINAMAL WORK DONE BY THIS ROUTINE.
                                   14472              *  WE CALL DEVICE DEPENDENT ROUTINES TO DO RENAME.
                                   14473              *  WE CALL DEVICE DEPENDENT ROUTINES AS FOLLOWS:
                                   14474              *    R1,R0 - OLD NAME LENGTH
                                   14475              *    R2,R3 - NEW NAME LENGTH
                                   14476              *    ON EXIT FFRNAME IS NEW FULLY RESOLVED NAME.
                                   14477              *    DEVICE ROUTINE PRINTS MESSAGE ABOUT RENAME.
                                   14478              *
                                   14479              *  NOTE,CAUTION!
                                   14480              *  THE RENAME IS A BIT GRIMY AND UNUSUAL IN THAT
                                   14481              *  IT HAS TO DEAL WITH 2 FILE NAMES. THE FILE NAME
                                   14482              *  SCANNING ROUTINES ARE NOT BUILT TO DO THAT. WE
                                   14483              *  THEREFORE TAKE SOME LIBERTIES WITH THE NAME
                                   14484              *  RESOLVING ROUTINES BY RESOLVING 2 FILE NAMES.
                                   14485              *  I THINK THIS IS OK, BUT IT IS NOT AN EXPECTED
                                   14486              *  USE OF THESE FILE SCANING/NAME RESOLVING ROUTINES.
                                   14487              *
                                   14488              *  NOTE:
                                   14489              *  THE OLD FILE NAME DETERMINES THE FILE TYPE.
                                   14490              *  THE FILE OPTIONS (EG. USER) ARE APPLIED TO BOTH
                                   14491              *  OLD AND NEW FILE NAMES BY NAME RESOLVE ROUTINE.
                                   14492              *  SEE ABOVE COMMENTS.
                                   14493              *
                                   14494              *
 000000                00000 00300 14495              RNWA     RECORD BEGIN
 000000                            14503  1           RNCMDL     DS    F
                                   14504  1           RNCMD      DS    CL(&LINESZ)
 000004                                   1          +RNCMD      DS    CL(235)
 0000F0                            14505  1           RNNEWL     DS    F                   NEW NAME
 0000F4                            14506  1           RNNEW      DS    CL(L'FFNAME)
 000174                            14507  1           RNRNEWL    DS    F                   FULL RESOLVED NEW NAME
 000178                            14508  1           RNRNEW     DS    CL(L'FFNAME)
 0001F8                            14509  1           RNOLDL     DS    F                   OLD NAME
 0001FC                            14510  1           RNOLD      DS    CL(L'FFNAME)
 00027C                            14511  1           RNROLDL    DS    F                   FULL RESOLVED OLD NAME
 000280                            14512  1           RNROLD     DS    CL(L'FFNAME)
 000300                00300 00300 14513                       END

0                                  19096              *
                                   19097              *
                                   19098              *  MKFFINFO - CREATE (MAKE) AND INITIALIZE A FFINFO
                                   19099              *        DSECT WORK AREA ON THE HEAP.
                                   19100              *
                                   19101              *  ON EXIT:
                                   19102              *    CPFINFOP - CONTAINS ADDRESS OF THE FFINFO DSECT
                                   19103              *
                                   19104              *  NOTE:
                                   19105              *  THIS ROUTINE MAY BE CALLED MULTIPLE TIMES, ONLY
                                   19106              *  ONE DSECT WILL BE CREATED.  THIS IS SO IF ONE
                                   19107              *  CAN BE AUTOMATICALLY OR EXPLICITLY CREATED FOR THE
                                   19108              *  CALLING ROUTINES.
                                   19109              *
                                   19110              *  THE DSECT IS INITIALIZED TO ZEROS. WITH THE EXCEPTION
                                   19111              *  THAT THE PREVIOUS FILE NAME/HOST/TYPE IS SAVED IS THE
                                   19112              *  WORKAREA.  (NOTE; THE PREVIOUS REALLY IS THE CURRENT
                                   19113              *  FILE NAME/HOST/TYPE. BUT IT MAY SOON BE PREVIOUS IF
                                   19114              *  THIS IS A 'USE XYZ ..' COMMAND)
                                   19115              *
                                   19116              *
 002FE8 50E0 D000/9008_      00000 19117              MKFFINFO XPROC ,
 USING  *,R7
                                   19157
                                   19158                       COMMENT                   IF NEEDED, MAKE FFINFO DSECT
 003002 D503 71EA BE54_031EC 00E54 19159                       IF    (CPFINFOP,EQ,0),BEGIN
                                   19177  1
                                   19178  1                      COMMENT                   GET HEAP SPACE
 00300C 5800 71EE            031F0 19179  1                      L     R0,=A(L'FFINFO)
 003010 58E0 71F2/0DEE       031F4 19180  1                      VCALL GETHEAP
 003016 5010 BE54            00E54 19184  1                      ST    R1,CPFINFOP
                                   19185  1
 00301A 1861                       19186  1                      LR    R6,R1
 USING  FFINFO,R6                  19187  1                      USING FFINFO,R6
                                   19196  1
                                   19197  1                      COMMENT                   INITIALIZE
 00301C 4120 6000            00000 19198  1                      LA    R2,FFINFO
 003020 4130 03A0            003A0 19199  1                      LA    R3,L'FFINFO
 003024 1B55                       19200  1                      CLEAR R5
 003026 0E24                       19204  1                      MVCL  R2,R4               CLEAR FFINFO DSECT
                                   19205  1                      COMMENT                   SET PREVIOUS FILE NAME/HOST/TYPE
 003028 D200 6003 B626 00003 00626 19206  1                      MVC   FFPTYPE,CPAFTYPE
 00302E D203 6298 B628 00298 00628 19207  1                      MVC   FFPNAMEL,CPAFNAMEL
 003034 D27F 629C B62C 0029C 0062C 19208  1                      MVC   FFPNAME,CPAFNAME
 00303A D203 631C B6AC 0031C 006AC 19209  1                      MVC   FFPHOSTL,CPAHOSTL
 003040 D27F 6320 B6B0 00320 006B0 19210  1                      MVC   FFPHOST,CPAHOST
                                   19211  1
 003046                            19212                       END   , NEED NEW FFINFO DSECT
                                   19216
 003046 18D8/9808 D004_            19217                       PEND  ,
 DROP   *,R7

0                                  19511              *
                                   19512              *
                                   19513              *  FNAMESCN - SCAN FILE NAME
                                   19514              *
                                   19515              *  ENTERED AS SCKW PROCESSING ROUTINE. EG. --
                                   19516              *  SCKW FROM,V(DSNSCAN)
                                   19517              *  -- WE SCAN AND SAVE THE NAME.
                                   19518              *
                                   19519              *  ON ENTRY:
                                   19520              *    SCAN CONTROL BLOCK POINTS TO FILE NAME TO SCAN
                                   19521              *
                                   19522              *  ON EXIT:
                                   19523              *    IF ERROR, R15=NZ, AND ERROR MSG PUT IN SCAN CONTROL BLOCK
                                   19524              *
                                   19525              *
                                   19526              *

0                                  23259              ¿þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþÜ
                                   23260              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   23261              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   23262              Ÿ  FNAMEFIN - FINISH FILE NAME PROCESSING.                            Ÿ
                                   23263              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   23264              Ÿ  THE PURPOSE OF THIS ROUTINE IS TO DETERMINE THE                    Ÿ
                                   23265              Ÿ  FILE SYSTEM TYPE.  (IE. FIND OUT WHICH TYPE OF FILE                Ÿ
                                   23266              Ÿ  OPEN TO DO.)  WE THEN PASS ALL THE FILE NAME AND                   Ÿ
                                   23267              Ÿ  OPTIONS TO THE APPROPRIATE OPEN ROUTINE AND LET                    Ÿ
                                   23268              Ÿ  THAT ROUTINE FIGURE OUT WHAT TO DO.                                Ÿ
                                   23269              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   23270              Ÿ  THIS ROUTINE ALSO APPLIES SOME ZAP TYPE LOGIC.                     Ÿ
                                   23271              Ÿ  WE WANT ALL FILE NAMES TO BE OF THE FORM                           Ÿ
                                   23272              Ÿ    <file name> [on <host>] [file type]                              Ÿ
                                   23273              Ÿ  SO WE FIX ALL REFERENCES TO 'on <ibm volume>' TO BE                Ÿ
                                   23274              Ÿ  THE SAME AS 'WINGS VOL=<ibm volume>' AND SAMSON                    Ÿ
                                   23275              Ÿ  FILENAMES C:NAME TO BE 'C:NAME SAMSON'.  IN SHORT                  Ÿ
                                   23276              Ÿ  THERE IS SOME LOGIC TO MAKE OLD STUFF CONFORM TO                   Ÿ
                                   23277              Ÿ  THE NEW.  THEN WE DO OUR THING WHICH IS TO FIND THE                Ÿ
                                   23278              Ÿ  FILE SYSTEM TYPE.                                                  Ÿ
                                   23279              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   23280              Ÿ  WE DETERMINE FILE SYSTEM TYPE AS FOLLOWS:                          Ÿ
                                   23281              Ÿ   1. FILE SYSTEM EXPLICITLY SET                                     Ÿ
                                   23282              Ÿ   2. ZAP ROUTINES IMPLY OLD FORMAT OLDIBM/WINGS/SAMSON              Ÿ
                                   23283              Ÿ   3. 'ON <HOST>' IMPLIES NET                                        Ÿ
                                   23284              Ÿ   4. '*' IMPLIES USE CURRENT FILE TYPE                              Ÿ
                                   23285              Ÿ   4. USE DEFAULT FILE TYPE                                          Ÿ
                                   23286              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   23287              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                                      ¾þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþ»
